74.3(1): lho phyogs mi bced 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sems can thar par drangs so/ /de ltar 
74.4(1): bde bar gshegs pa thabs mkhas la thugs rje che ba/ bskal pa bzang po'i sangs 
74.5(1): rgyas gnyis brgya de ni/ nyon mongs pa med cing zag pa zad pa/ ting 'dzin snyoms 
74.6(1): shing gzungs dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa rig pa dang stobs shugs su ldan 
74.7(1): cing / nyon mongs pa'i dgra 'dul ba/ sems can gyi don la 'od zer yongs su spro 
74.8(1): zhing 'dul ba'i zhing khams la phyogs ris med pa/ thabs dang thugs rjes lho phyogs 
74.9(1): mi bced 'jig rten gyi khams/ / de dag gi ris drug 'khor ba'i sems can rnams 
74.10(1): la/ thugs rjes yongs su drangs zhing / bon nyid bde ba'i gnas su bkod pa'i 
74.11(1): bde bar gshegs pa gnyis brgya pa de ni/ sku'i mtshan nyid thog ma la yab yum gyi 
74.12(1): le'u dang / sku'i skyes rabs dang bam po brgyad pa le'u dgu pa'o// //
74.13(1): 7 rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku la phyag 'tshal lo/ /yang bde bar gshegs 
74.14(1): pa thabs mkhas la thugs rje che ba'i/ gto rgyal ye mkhyen gyi sku'i sprul pa la/ bskal 
74.15(1): pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas gnyis brgya byon te/ lha ye lha kun tu bzang po dang / srid 
74.16(1): pa ye mu rgyung dkar po gnyis kyi byin gyis brlabs te/ dbus phyogs bde ba'i zhing 
74.17(1): khams mtha' dbus kun 'dzom grong khyer gling / skye 'gro 'dul sogs mi bced pa'i 
74.18(1): yul/ grong khyer 'od bdal ljon phyug gi gling la spros te/ lha de rnams kyis kyang 
74.19(1): thugs rjes 'od spros nas/ yul khams de dag gi sems can thar par drangs nas/
74.20(1): bon nyid kyi dbyings su bkod do/ /yang bde bar gshegs pa mi 'gyur rin chen 
74.21(1): gtsugs gi rgyan zhes bya ba de ni/ dbus phyogs grong khyer 'od bdal ljon phyug gi 
75.1(1): gling la sku 'khrungs te/ yab ni 'od lha bdud 'dul dkar po zhes bya ba lags so/ /
75.2(1): yum ni lha mo g.yu mdzes 'od 'khyil ma zhes bya ba lags so/ /yab yum de gnyis 
75.3(1): sprul pa'i sras su skyes te/ sras de ni ngo mtshar dpe' byad yongs su 'dzom pa ni/ na 
75.4(1): 'dam nang gi me tog ud du 'bar ba dang 'dra'o/ /sku mtshan legs pa'i dpe' 
75.5(1): byad ni shin tu bzang la/ gsung dbyangs tshangs pa'i khu byug ltar lhang lhang sgrogs 
75.6(1): so/ /yul khams de dag gi sems can la bon ston zhing sku la 'od zer mang po spros 
75.7(1): so/ /'gro ba sems can la char sbyin phab pa'o/ /ston pa de yis 'dul ba'i zhing 
75.8(1): khams las kyang / bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag du ma bsam las 'das te/ de dag 
75.9(1): gi sems can gyi las dkar nag kyang tshad dang bsam la 'das so/ /de dag gi 
75.10(1): 'dren pa'i sdongs dang ston pa la/ bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas lnga bcu byon te/
75.11(1): lha 'chi med tshe yi rgyal po zhes bya ba dang / lha g.yung drung sku dang ldan pa zhes bya ba 
75.12(1): dang / lha a dkar thig le bdag nyid ces bya ba dang / lha me tog sna tshogs kyi 
75.13(1): gdugs 'dzin zhes bya ba dang / lha 'bar ba'i gtsug gtor can zhes bya ba dang /
75.14(1): lha byi ru dmar po'i gting mdangs zhes bya ba dang / lha gzi 'od yong bkra zhes bya 
75.15(1): ba dang / lha pad ma'i 'phreng ba 'dzin zhes bya ba dang / lha nor bu'i tog rtol zhes 
75.16(1): bya ba dang / lha 'od dkar po'i gdugs bdal pa zhes bya ba dang / lha ka dkar 
75.17(1): po'i gdugs bdal pa zhes bya ba dang / lha thing nams spang la nam rgyas zhes bya ba 
75.18(1): dang / lha bsrid pa'i ding bkra 'od legs zhes bya ba dang / lha legs pa'i sgron ma 
75.19(1): zhes bya ba dang / lha thing nams gsal zhes bya ba dang / lha mu rgyas yongs spro zhes bya 
75.20(1): ba dang / lha thugs rje dam pa gser gyi snying po zhes bya ba dang / lha yid bzhin 'od 
75.21(1): 'bar ba'i zer dang ldan zhes bya ba dang / de ltar bde bar gshegs pa'i lha bco 
76.1(1): brgyad pa de ni/ dbus phyogs kun 'dul bde ba'i gling la sku 'khrungs te/ yab ni 
76.2(1): kun bdal dam pa'i gtsug ces bya'o/ /yum ni gser sbyin ma zhes bya ba dang /

76.5(1): legs so/ /la la ngo mtshar gsung gi bkod pa ni shin tu bzang ngo / /la la thugs 
76.6(1): bskyed rnam par dag pa'i ting 'dzin gyis/ 'gro ba sems can la byang chub mchog

76.13(1): sems can yongs la sbyin pa zhes bya ba dang / lha me 'od tog dkar po zhes bya ba 
76.14(1): dang / lha sbyin 'od yongs kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba dang / lha rgyan rnams sna tshogs du ma

76.18(1): ces bya ba dang / lha rin po che'i dbyugs pa 'dzin zhes bya ba dang / lha gser gyi
